mahyaṃ namantāṃ pradiśaś catasras tvayādhyakṣeṇa pṛtanā jayema | [MS, 1, 4, 1 1.2]
agne vratapate vratam ālapsye tat te prabrūmas tan no gopāya tañ śakeyam | [MS, 1, 4, 1 2.1]
agniṃ hotāram upa taṃ huve devān yajñiyān iha yānyajāmahai | [MS, 1, 4, 1 3.1]
vyantu devā haviṣo me asyā devā yantu sumanasyamānāḥ | [MS, 1, 4, 1 3.2]
yunajmi tvā brahmaṇā daivyena havyāyāsmai voḍhave jātavedaḥ | [MS, 1, 4, 1 4.1]
indhānās tvā suprajasaḥ suvīrā jyog jīvema balihṛto vayaṃ te | [MS, 1, 4, 1 4.2]

asmākaṃ santv āśiṣaḥ | [MS, 1, 4, 1 5.2]
ām āśiṣo dohakāmā indravanto havāmahe | [MS, 1, 4, 1 6.1]
dhukṣīmahi prajām iṣam | [MS, 1, 4, 1 6.2]
sā me satyāśīr devān gamyājjuṣṭāj juṣṭatarā paṇyāt paṇyatarā | [MS, 1, 4, 1 7.1]
areḍatā manasā devān gaccha yajño devān gacchatu yajño devān gamyāt | [MS, 1, 4, 1 8.1]
vi te muñcāmi raśanāṃ vi raśmīn vi yoktrāṇi paricartanāni | [MS, 1, 4, 1 9.1]
dhattād asmabhyaṃ draviṇeha bhadraṃ pra mā brūtād bhāgadāṃ devatāsu | [MS, 1, 4, 1 9.2]
iṣṭo yajño bhṛgubhir draviṇodā yatibhir āśīrdā vasubhiḥ | [MS, 1, 4, 1 10.1]
aṅgiraso me asya yajñasya prātaranuvākair ahauṣuḥ | [MS, 1, 4, 1 10.2]
tasya mā yajñasyeṣṭasya vītasya draviṇehāgamyād vasur yajño vasumān yajñas tasya mā yajñasya vasor vasumato vasv ihāgacchatv ado māgacchatv ado māgamyāt | [MS, 1, 4, 1 11.1]

aganma svaḥ | [MS, 1, 4, 2 21]

{MS, 1, 4, 3}
ye devā yajñahanaḥ pṛthivyām adhy āsate | [MS, 1, 4, 3 1.1]

tān eva bhrātṛvyād yuvate | [MS, 1, 10, 8 25]

{MS, 1, 10, 10}

ye madhyamās tam agnaye dātre 'ṣṭākapālaṃ nirvapet | [MS, 2, 2, 13 2]
ye sthaviṣṭhās tam indrāya pradātre dadhaṃś carum | [MS, 2, 2, 13 3]
ye kṣodiṣṭhās taṃ viṣṇave śipiviṣṭāya śṛte carum | [MS, 2, 2, 13 4]
agnir vai madhyamasya dātā | [MS, 2, 2, 13 5]
indro jyeṣṭhasya pradātā | [MS, 2, 2, 13 6]
atha yat kṣodiṣṭhaṃ tañ śipiviṣṭam | [MS, 2, 2, 13 7]
tad āpnoti | [MS, 2, 2, 13 8]
paśūn eva | [MS, 2, 2, 13 9]
somo vā etasyātiricyate yasya sānnāyyaṃ candramā abhyudeti | [MS, 2, 2, 13 10]
sa vai paśūn evābhyatiricyate | [MS, 2, 2, 13 11]
yaḥ paśukāmaḥ syāt so 'māvāsyām iṣṭvā vatsān apākuryāt | [MS, 2, 2, 13 12]
ye puroḍāśyāḥ syus tāṃs tredhā kuryāt | [MS, 2, 2, 13 13]
ye kṣodiṣṭhās tam agnaye sanimate 'ṣṭākapālaṃ nirvapet | [MS, 2, 2, 13 14]
ye madhyamās taṃ viṣṇave śipiviṣṭāya śṛte carum | [MS, 2, 2, 13 15]
ye sthaviṣṭhās tam indrāya pradātre dadhaṃś carum | [MS, 2, 2, 13 16]
agnir evāsmai tad vindati yad iha | [MS, 2, 2, 13 17]
viṣṇus tad yad antarikṣe | [MS, 2, 2, 13 18]
indras tad yad divi | [MS, 2, 2, 13 19]
satvāno gā icchanti | [MS, 2, 2, 13 20]
yad ete taṇḍulā vibhājyante | [MS, 2, 2, 13 21]
satvāno vā eta eṣṭāraḥ | [MS, 2, 2, 13 22]
abhiroddhāra eva | [MS, 2, 2, 13 23]
āgneyam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvaped gataśrīḥ | [MS, 2, 2, 13 24]
tasya gaur dhenur dakṣiṇā | [MS, 2, 2, 13 25]
sa prāṅ prayāya vaiṣṇavaṃ trikapālam | [MS, 2, 2, 13 26]
tasya vaḍabā dhenur dakṣiṇā | [MS, 2, 2, 13 27]
sa prāṅ prayāya giriṃ gatvāpo vā prājāpatyaṃ ghṛte carum | [MS, 2, 2, 13 28]
tasya puruṣī dhenur dakṣiṇā | [MS, 2, 2, 13 29]
yad āgneya imāṃ tenākramate | [MS, 2, 2, 13 30]
yad vaiṣṇavo 'ntarikṣaṃ tena | [MS, 2, 2, 13 31]
yat prājāpatyo 'muṃ tena lokam | [MS, 2, 2, 13 32]
yat prāṅ prayāty abhi svid evākramīt | [MS, 2, 2, 13 33]
yad giriṃ gacchaty apo vāntaṃ svid evāgan | [MS, 2, 2, 13 34]
yat tisro dhenavo dakṣiṇā | [MS, 2, 2, 13 35]
trayo vā ime lokāḥ | [MS, 2, 2, 13 36]
imān asmai lokān dhenur akaḥ | [MS, 2, 2, 13 37]
imān asmai lokān pradāpayati | [MS, 2, 2, 13 38]
prattān ha vā asmā imāṃl lokān duhe ya evaṃ veda | [MS, 2, 2, 13 39]
saumendraṃ caruṃ nirvapeñ śyāmākaṃ somavāmine | [MS, 2, 2, 13 40]
indro vai tvaṣṭuḥ somam apibad anupahūyamānaḥ | [MS, 2, 2, 13 41]
tasyordhvaḥ somapītho 'patat | [MS, 2, 2, 13 42]
te śyāmākā abhavan | [MS, 2, 2, 13 43]
somapīthena vā eṣa vyṛdhyate yaḥ somaṃ vamiti | [MS, 2, 2, 13 44]
yat saumyaḥ | [MS, 2, 2, 13 45]
somapīthenaivainaṃ samardhayati | [MS, 2, 2, 13 46]
indriyeṇa vā eṣa vīryeṇa vyṛdhyate yaḥ somaṃ vamiti | [MS, 2, 2, 13 47]
yad aindraḥ | [MS, 2, 2, 13 48]
indriyeṇaivainaṃ vīryeṇa samardhayati | [MS, 2, 2, 13 49]
śithira iva hi vā etasya somapīthaḥ | [MS, 2, 2, 13 50]
athaiṣa somaṃ vamiti | [MS, 2, 2, 13 51]
yañ śyāmākataṇḍulaiḥ śrīṇāti somapīthasya dhṛtyai | [MS, 2, 2, 13 52]
{MS, 2, 3, 1}
āgneyam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvapen maitrāvaruṇīṃ payasyām | [MS, 2, 3, 1 1]
āmayāvinaṃ yājayet | [MS, 2, 3, 1 2]
ṛddhyā evāgneyaḥ | [MS, 2, 3, 1 3]
atho asthanvantam evainaṃ kṛtvā pratiṣṭhāpayati | [MS, 2, 3, 1 4]
īśvarā vai payasyā ṛte paśor aśāntā nirmṛjaḥ | [MS, 2, 3, 1 5]
paśur apy ālabhyaḥ | [MS, 2, 3, 1 6]
śāntyā anirmārgāya | [MS, 2, 3, 1 7]
ete vai paśavo yad vrīhayaś ca yavāś ca | [MS, 2, 3, 1 8]

śāntyā anirmārgāya | [MS, 2, 3, 1 10]
maitrāvaruṇī brāhmaṇasya syāt | [MS, 2, 3, 1 11]
maitrāvaruṇo hi brāhmaṇo devatayā | [MS, 2, 3, 1 12]
aindravāruṇī rājanyasya syāt | [MS, 2, 3, 1 13]

āgnivāruṇī vaiśyasya syāt | [MS, 2, 3, 1 15]
agnir vai sarvā devatāḥ | [MS, 2, 3, 1 16]
atra vaiśyasyāpi devatā | [MS, 2, 3, 1 17]
āmayāvinaṃ yājayet | [MS, 2, 3, 1 18]
svām eva devatāṃ prāyaścittyā upāsarat | [MS, 2, 3, 1 19]
varuṇagṛhīto vā eṣa ya āmayāvī | [MS, 2, 3, 1 20]
varuṇād evainaṃ tena muñcati | [MS, 2, 3, 1 21]
payo vai puruṣaḥ paya etasyāmayati | [MS, 2, 3, 1 22]
payasaivāsya payo niṣkrīṇāti | [MS, 2, 3, 1 23]
yad vyūhati | [MS, 2, 3, 1 24]
vikṛtya hi śalyaṃ madhyato nirharanti | [MS, 2, 3, 1 25]
tad yakṣmaṃ vāvāsyaitan madhyato nirharanti | [MS, 2, 3, 1 26]
atha yat punaḥ samuhyāgnaye samavadyati | [MS, 2, 3, 1 27]
yathā śalyaṃ nirhṛtyoṣṇīṣeṇa veṣṭayanty evaṃ tad bhūtikāmaṃ yājayet | [MS, 2, 3, 1 28]
svām eva devatāṃ prāyaścittyā upāsarat | [MS, 2, 3, 1 29]
varuṇagṛhīto vā eṣa yo bhūtikāmaḥ | [MS, 2, 3, 1 30]
varuṇād evainaṃ tena muñcati | [MS, 2, 3, 1 31]
payo vai puruṣaḥ | [MS, 2, 3, 1 32]
paya eṣa icchati yo bhūtim icchati | [MS, 2, 3, 1 33]
payasaivāsmai payo 'varunddhe | [MS, 2, 3, 1 34]
yad vyūhati | [MS, 2, 3, 1 35]
yajñasya gopīthāya | [MS, 2, 3, 1 36]
atha yat punaḥ samūhati | [MS, 2, 3, 1 37]
bhūtyaivainaṃ samūhati | [MS, 2, 3, 1 38]
grāmakāmaṃ yājayet | [MS, 2, 3, 1 39]
svām eva devatāṃ prāyaścittyā upāsarat | [MS, 2, 3, 1 40]
varuṇagṛhīto vā eṣa yo grāmakāmaḥ | [MS, 2, 3, 1 41]
varuṇād evainaṃ tena muñcati | [MS, 2, 3, 1 42]
payo vai puruṣaḥ | [MS, 2, 3, 1 43]
paya eṣa icchati yo grāmam icchati | [MS, 2, 3, 1 44]
payasaivāsmai payo 'varunddhe | [MS, 2, 3, 1 45]
yad vyūhati | [MS, 2, 3, 1 46]
yajñasya gopīthāya | [MS, 2, 3, 1 47]
atha yat punaḥ samūhati | [MS, 2, 3, 1 48]
grāmeṇaivainaṃ samūhati | [MS, 2, 3, 1 49]
ekakapālān juhoti | [MS, 2, 3, 1 50]
atrātra vai varuṇasya pāśāḥ | [MS, 2, 3, 1 51]
tata enaṃ muñcati | [MS, 2, 3, 1 52]
yan nānā juhuyād vikarṣaḥ sa yajñasya | [MS, 2, 3, 1 53]
agnau sarve hotavyāḥ | [MS, 2, 3, 1 54]
samṛddhyai | [MS, 2, 3, 1 55]
yā vāṃ mitrāvaruṇā ojasyā tanūs tayā vāṃ vidhema | [MS, 2, 3, 1 56]
tayemam amuṃ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ | [MS, 2, 3, 1 57]
yā vāṃ mitrāvaruṇau sahasyā tanūs tayā vāṃ vidhema | [MS, 2, 3, 1 58]
tayemam amuṃ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ | [MS, 2, 3, 1 59]

tayemam amuṃ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ | [MS, 2, 3, 1 61]

tayemam amuṃ muñcatam aṃhasaḥ | [MS, 2, 3, 1 63]

tasmai te svāhā | [MS, 2, 3, 1 71]
yas te rājan varuṇauṣadhīṣu vanaspatiṣv apsu pṛthivyāṃ dikṣu pāśas taṃ ta etenāvayaje | [MS, 2, 3, 1 72]

{MS, 2, 3, 2}
vaiśvadevaṃ caruṃ nirvaped bhrātṛvyavān | [MS, 2, 3, 2 1]
devāś ca vā asurāś cāspardhanta | [MS, 2, 3, 2 2]
te devāḥ saṃgrahaṇenāyajanta | [MS, 2, 3, 2 3]
te yat kiṃ cāsurāṇāṃ svam āsīt tat samagṛhṇan | [MS, 2, 3, 2 4]
manāṃsi vāvaiṣāṃ tat samagṛhṇan | [MS, 2, 3, 2 5]
te 'manasaḥ parābhavan | [MS, 2, 3, 2 6]
bhrātṛvyavān yajeta | [MS, 2, 3, 2 7]
manograhaṇaṃ vā etat | [MS, 2, 3, 2 8]
manāṃsi vā etad bhrātṛvyāṇāṃ saṃgṛhṇāti | [MS, 2, 3, 2 9]
te 'manasaḥ parābhavanti | [MS, 2, 3, 2 10]
grāmakāmo yajeta | [MS, 2, 3, 2 11]
manograhaṇaṃ vā etat | [MS, 2, 3, 2 12]

te 'smān manogṛhītā nāpayanti | [MS, 2, 3, 2 14]
sarveṣāṃ sajātānāṃ gṛhād ājyam āhareyuḥ | [MS, 2, 3, 2 15]

te 'smān manogṛhītā nāpayanti | [MS, 2, 3, 2 17]
āmanena juhoti | [MS, 2, 3, 2 18]
āmanasa evainān karoti | [MS, 2, 3, 2 19]

te māṃ kāmayantāṃ hṛdā | [MS, 2, 3, 2 21]
tān mā āmanasas kṛdhi svāhā | [MS, 2, 3, 2 22]

tān mā āmanasas kṛdhi svāhā | [MS, 2, 3, 2 25]

tā mā āmanasas kṛdhi svāhā | [MS, 2, 3, 2 28]

tān mā āmanasas kṛdhi svāhā | [MS, 2, 3, 2 31]

tair ātmānam abhisaṃyuṅkte | [MS, 2, 3, 2 33]
tair bhavati | [MS, 2, 3, 2 34]
pṛṣatī gaur dhenur dakṣiṇā | [MS, 2, 3, 2 35]
sā hi vaiśvadevī | [MS, 2, 3, 2 36]
atha yad vaiśvadevīṣṭiḥ | [MS, 2, 3, 2 37]
vaiśvadevīr vā imāḥ prajāḥ | [MS, 2, 3, 2 38]
tā evāvārunddha | [MS, 2, 3, 2 39]
tā ādyā akṛta | [MS, 2, 3, 2 40]
bahirātmaṃ vai prayājānuyājāḥ | [MS, 2, 3, 2 41]
ātmā devatā | [MS, 2, 3, 2 42]
yat prayājānuyājānāṃ purastād vopariṣṭād vā juhuyād bahirātmaṃ sajātān dadhīta | [MS, 2, 3, 2 43]
atha yan madhyato juhoti | [MS, 2, 3, 2 44]
madhyata eva sajātān ātman dhatte | [MS, 2, 3, 2 45]
yadi kāmayeta tājag eyuḥ | [MS, 2, 3, 2 46]

yadi kāmayeta dhruvāḥ syuḥ | [MS, 2, 3, 2 49]

dhruvā hīyam | [MS, 2, 3, 2 51]
dhruvo 'si | [MS, 2, 3, 2 52]
dhruvas tvaṃ deveṣv edhi | [MS, 2, 3, 2 53]

ugras tvaṃ deveṣv edhi | [MS, 2, 3, 2 56]

{MS, 2, 3, 3}
athaiṣo 'śvaḥ pratigṛhyate | [MS, 2, 3, 3 1]
sa vā ubhayatodan pratigṛhītaḥ | [MS, 2, 3, 3 2]
nirbabhasty asyendriyaṃ ca paśūṃś ca | [MS, 2, 3, 3 3]
varuṇo vā aśvo varuṇadevatyaḥ | [MS, 2, 3, 3 4]
yo vā aśvaṃ pratigṛhṇāti varuṇaṃ sa prasīdati | [MS, 2, 3, 3 5]
tad aśvahaviṣā yaṣṭavyam | [MS, 2, 3, 3 6]
nirvaruṇatvāya | [MS, 2, 3, 3 7]
catuṣkapālā bhavanti | [MS, 2, 3, 3 8]
catuṣpād vā aśvaḥ | [MS, 2, 3, 3 9]
kapālair evainam āpnoti | [MS, 2, 3, 3 10]
yāvanto 'śvās tāvantaḥ puroḍāśā bhavanti | [MS, 2, 3, 3 11]
sarvata evainaṃ muñcati | [MS, 2, 3, 3 12]
eko 'dhi bhavati | [MS, 2, 3, 3 13]
yan nopasmarati tasmā eva sa | [MS, 2, 3, 3 14]
yaḥ punaḥ pratigrahiṣyant syān na sa yajeta | [MS, 2, 3, 3 15]
yaddhi punaḥ pratigṛhṇīyāt punar varuṇaṃ prasīdet | [MS, 2, 3, 3 16]

yad vāruṇo varuṇād evainaṃ tena muñcati | [MS, 2, 3, 3 18]
atha yat sauryaḥ | [MS, 2, 3, 3 19]
svām eva devatām upapratigṛhṇāti | [MS, 2, 3, 3 20]
ātmano 'hiṃsāyai | [MS, 2, 3, 3 21]
ekaviṃśatiḥ sāmidhenīr bhavanti | [MS, 2, 3, 3 22]
asā āditya ekaviṃśaḥ | [MS, 2, 3, 3 23]
prajāpatir asā ādityaḥ | [MS, 2, 3, 3 24]
prājāpatyo 'śvaḥ | [MS, 2, 3, 3 25]
yāvān evāśvas tam āpnoti | [MS, 2, 3, 3 26]
sarve vā anye paśavo yonimantaḥ puruṣayonayaḥ | [MS, 2, 3, 3 27]
ayonir aśvo 'psujāḥ | [MS, 2, 3, 3 28]
yad eṣo 'ponaptrīyaś carur bhavati | [MS, 2, 3, 3 29]
yonimantam evainam akaḥ | [MS, 2, 3, 3 30]
sva evainaṃ yonau pratiṣṭhāpayati | [MS, 2, 3, 3 31]
yas te rājan varuṇa gāyatracchandāḥ pāśo brahman pratiṣṭhitas taṃ ta etenāvayaje | [MS, 2, 3, 3 32]
tasmai te svāhā | [MS, 2, 3, 3 33]
yas te rājan varuṇa triṣṭupcchandāḥ pāśaḥ kṣatre pratiṣṭhitas taṃ ta etenāvayaje | [MS, 2, 3, 3 34]
tasmai te svāhā | [MS, 2, 3, 3 35]

yair enaṃ gṛhṇāti tair enaṃ muñcati | [MS, 2, 3, 3 42]
aponaptrīyābhyāṃ dvābhyāṃ juhoti | [MS, 2, 3, 3 43]

tenāsmā amuṣmā āyur dehi | [MS, 2, 3, 4 2.1]

{MS, 2, 7, 14}

agnir no vanate rayim | [MS, 2, 10, 2 1.2]

{MS, 2, 10, 3}

teṣām iṣṭāni sam iṣā madanti yatrā saptaṛṣīn para ekam āhuḥ | [MS, 2, 10, 3 2.2]
ta āyajanta draviṇā sam asminn ṛṣayaḥ pūrve jaritāro na bhūnā | [MS, 2, 10, 3 2.3]
asūrtā sūrte rajasi niṣattā ye bhūtāni samakṛṇvann imāni | [MS, 2, 10, 3 2.4]
yo naḥ pitā janitā yo vidhartā yo naḥ sato abhy ā saj jajāna | [MS, 2, 10, 3 3.1]
yo devānāṃ nāmadhā eka eva taṃ saṃpraśnaṃ bhuvanā yanty anyā | [MS, 2, 10, 3 3.2]
paro divaḥ para enā pṛthivyāḥ paro devebhyo asuraṃ yad asti | [MS, 2, 10, 3 4.1]
kaṃ svid garbhaṃ prathamaṃ dadhrā āpo yatra devāḥ samagacchanta sarve | [MS, 2, 10, 3 4.2]
tam id garbhaṃ prathamaṃ dadhrā āpo yatra devāḥ samapaśyanta viśve | [MS, 2, 10, 3 4.3]

{MS, 3, 11, 1}

{MS, 3, 15, 1}
śādaṃ dadbhir avakān dantamūlair mṛdaṃ barsvai stegān daṃṣṭrābhyām avakrandena tālu vājaṃ hanubhyāṃ sarasvatyā agrajihvaṃ jihvāyā utsādam apa āsyena vṛṣaṇā āṇḍābhyām ādityāñ śmaśrubhiḥ panthāṃ bhrūbhyāṃ dyāvāpṛthivī vartobhyāṃ vidyutaṃ kanīnikābhyāṃ karṇābhyāṃ śrotre śrotrābhyāṃ karṇā avāryāṇi pakṣmāṇi pāryā ikṣavaḥ pāryāṇi pakṣmāṇy avāryā ikṣavaḥ | [MS, 3, 15, 1 1]
{MS, 3, 15, 7}
indrasya kroḍo 'dityāḥ pājasyaṃ diśāṃ jatravo 'dityā bhasad jīmūtān hṛdayaupaśābhyām antarikṣaṃ pulītatā nabha udaryeṇa valmīkān klomnā glaubhir gulmāṃś cakravākau matasnābhyāṃ divaṃ vṛkkābhyāṃ hirābhiḥ sravantīr girīn plāśibhyām upalān plīhnā hradān kukṣibhyāṃ samudram udareṇa vaiśvānaraṃ bhasmanā | [MS, 3, 15, 7 1]
{MS, 3, 16, 1}
mā no mitro varuṇo aryamāyur indra ṛbhukṣā marutaḥ parikśan | [MS, 3, 16, 1 1.1]

anv enaṃ viprā ṛṣayo madanti devānāṃ puṣṭe cakṛmā subandhum | [MS, 3, 16, 1 5.2]
hotādhvaryur āvayā agnimindho grāvagrābha uta śaṃstā suvipraḥ | [MS, 3, 16, 1 6.1]
tena yajñena svaraṃkṛtena sviṣṭena vakṣaṇā āpṛṇadhvam | [MS, 3, 16, 1 6.2]
yūpavraskā uta ye yūpavāhāś caṣālaṃ ye aśvayūpāya takṣati | [MS, 3, 16, 1 7.1]
ye cārvate pacanaṃ saṃbharanty uto teṣām abhigūrtir na invatu | [MS, 3, 16, 1 7.2]
yad vājino dāma saṃdānam arvato yā śīrṣaṇyā raśanā rajjur asya | [MS, 3, 16, 1 8.1]
yad vā ghāsya prabhṛtam āsye tṛṇaṃ sarvā tā te api deveṣv astu | [MS, 3, 16, 1 8.2]
yad ūvadhyam udarasyāpavāti ya āmasya kraviṣo gandho asti | [MS, 3, 16, 1 9.1]
sukṛtā tañ śamitāraḥ kṛṇvantūta medhaṃ śṛtapākaṃ pacantu | [MS, 3, 16, 1 9.2]
yad aśvasya kraviṣo makṣikāśa yad vā svarau svadhitau ripram asti | [MS, 3, 16, 1 10.1]
yaddhastayoḥ śamitur yan nakheṣu sarvā tā te api deveṣv astu | [MS, 3, 16, 1 10.2]
yat te gātrād agninā pacyamānād abhi śūlaṃ nihatasyāvadhāvati | [MS, 3, 16, 1 11.1]
mā tad bhūmyām āśriṣan mā tṛṇeṣu devebhyas tad uśadbhyo rātam astu | [MS, 3, 16, 1 11.2]
ye vājinaṃ paripaśyanti pakvaṃ ya īm āhuḥ surabhir nirhareti | [MS, 3, 16, 1 12.1]
ye cārvato māṃsabhikṣām upāsate uto teṣām abhigūrtir na invatu | [MS, 3, 16, 1 12.2]
yan nīkṣaṇaṃ māṃspacanyā ukhāyā yā pātrāṇi yūṣṇa āsecanāni | [MS, 3, 16, 1 13.1]
ūṣmaṇyāpidhānā carūṇām aṅkāḥ sūnāḥ paribhūṣanty aśvam | [MS, 3, 16, 1 13.2]
yad aśvāya vāsa upastṛṇanty adhivāsaṃ yā hiraṇyāny asmai | [MS, 3, 16, 1 14.1]
saṃdānam arvantaṃ paḍvīśaṃ priyā deveṣv āyāmayanti | [MS, 3, 16, 1 14.2]
nikramaṇaṃ niṣadanaṃ vivartanaṃ yac ca paḍvīśam arvataḥ | [MS, 3, 16, 1 15.1]
yac ca papau yac ca ghāsiṃ jaghāsa sarvā tā te api deveṣv astu | [MS, 3, 16, 1 15.2]
mā tvāgnir dhanayīd dhūmagandhir mokhā bhrājanty abhivikta jaghriḥ | [MS, 3, 16, 1 16.1]

{MS, 3, 16, 2}

etā u vaḥ subhagā viśvavārā vi pakṣobhiḥ śrayamāṇā ud ātaiḥ | [MS, 3, 16, 2 5.1]
ṛṣvāḥ satīḥ kavaṣaḥ śumbhamānā dvāro devīḥ suprāyaṇā bhavantu | [MS, 3, 16, 2 5.2]
antarā mitrāvaruṇā carantī mukhaṃ yajñānām abhi saṃvidāne | [MS, 3, 16, 2 6.1]

apiprayaṃ codanā vāṃ mimānā hotārā jyotiḥ pradiśā diśantā | [MS, 3, 16, 2 7.2]

{MS, 3, 16, 3}

rocante rocanā divi | [MS, 3, 16, 3 1.2]
yuñjanty asya kāmyā harī vipakṣasā rathe | [MS, 3, 16, 3 2.1]
śoṇā dhṛṣṇū nṛvāhasā | [MS, 3, 16, 3 2.2]
ketuṃ kṛṇvann aketave peśo maryā apeśase | [MS, 3, 16, 3 3.1]
sam uṣadbhir ajāyathāḥ | [MS, 3, 16, 3 3.2]

{MS, 3, 16, 4}

agniś ca havyavāhano bhavataṃ dāśuṣe mayaḥ | [MS, 3, 16, 4 13.2]
anv id anumate tvaṃ manyāsai śaṃ ca nas kṛdhi | [MS, 3, 16, 4 14.1]
kratve dakṣāya no hinu pra nā āyūṃṣi tāriṣat | [MS, 3, 16, 4 14.2]

agnir ukthena vāhasā | [MS, 3, 16, 4 15.2]
pṛṣṭo divi | [MS, 3, 16, 4 16.1]

{MS, 3, 16, 5}

staumīndraṃ nāthito johavīmi sa no muñcatv aṃhasaḥ | [MS, 3, 16, 5 4.2]

yā rājānā sarathaṃ yāta ugrā tā no muñcatam āgasaḥ | [MS, 3, 16, 5 5.2]

upa śreṣṭhā na āśiro devayor dharmā asthiran | [MS, 3, 16, 5 8.1]

marutāṃ manve adhi no bruvantu premāṃ vācaṃ viśvām avantu viśve | [MS, 3, 16, 5 11.1]
āśūn huve suyamān ūtaye te no muñcantv enasaḥ | [MS, 3, 16, 5 11.2]

staumi devān maruto nāthito johavīmi te no muñcantv enasaḥ | [MS, 3, 16, 5 12.2]

āśūn huve suyamān ūtaye te no muñcantv enasaḥ | [MS, 3, 16, 5 13.2]

staumi viśvān devān nāthito johavīmi te no muñcantv enasaḥ | [MS, 3, 16, 5 14.2]
anv adya no anumatiḥ | [MS, 3, 16, 5 15.1]

vaiśvānaro na ūtyā | [MS, 3, 16, 5 15.3]

{MS, 4, 4, 1}

yat tasya gṛhṇāti yaḥ pratīpaṃ yudhyaty ojasā vā eṣa vīryeṇa pratīpaṃ yudhyati | [MS, 4, 4, 1 2]
ojasā vā etad vīryeṇa rāṣṭra ojo vīryaṃ dadhāti | [MS, 4, 4, 1 3]
atha yat tasya gṛhṇāti yo 'nvīpam īrayati māhiṣaṃ tena tokaṃ prajanayati | [MS, 4, 4, 1 4]
atha yan nadīpater apāṃ vā etan mithunam | [MS, 4, 4, 1 5]
apāṃ vā etan mithunena rāṣṭre mithunaṃ dadhāti | [MS, 4, 4, 1 6]
atha yad aprahāvarīṇāṃ madhyameṣṭheyaṃ tenāvarunddhe | [MS, 4, 4, 1 7]
atha yat parivāhiṇīnāṃ pārevasyantyās tena tokaṃ prajanayati | [MS, 4, 4, 1 8]
atha yā āpo 'ñśerāḥ | [MS, 4, 4, 1 9]
ojasā vā etā vīryeṇāpo 'ñśerāḥ | [MS, 4, 4, 1 10]
ojasā vā etad vīryeṇa rāṣṭra ojo vīryaṃ dadhāti | [MS, 4, 4, 1 11]
atha yat kūpyānām ubhayīs tenāpo 'varunddhe | [MS, 4, 4, 1 12]
yāś ca samudriyā yāś cāsamudriyā īśvarā vā etam etā srotasyā āpo 'śāntā nirmṛjaḥ | [MS, 4, 4, 1 13]
yat sthāvarāṇāṃ gṛhṇāti śāntyā anirmārgāya | [MS, 4, 4, 1 14]
yā ātapati varṣati yāś ca paridadṛśre tā āpo brahmavarcasyāḥ | [MS, 4, 4, 1 15]
tābhī rāṣṭre brahmavarcasaṃ dadhāti | [MS, 4, 4, 1 16]
atha yaddhrādunīnāṃ viśas tena vīryam avarunddhe | [MS, 4, 4, 1 17]
atha yat puṣpāṇām āraṇyaṃ tena | [MS, 4, 4, 1 18]
atha yad ulbyānāṃ vajro vai paśavaḥ | [MS, 4, 4, 1 19]
vajrā ulbyāḥ | [MS, 4, 4, 1 20]
vajreṇa vā etad rāṣṭre vajraṃ dadhāti | [MS, 4, 4, 1 21]
atha yat payasaḥ payasā vā etad rāṣṭre payo dadhāti | [MS, 4, 4, 1 22]
atha yad ghṛtasyaitā vā āpo 'nādhṛṣyāḥ | [MS, 4, 4, 1 23]
tābhī rāṣṭram anādhṛṣyaṃ karoti | [MS, 4, 4, 1 24]
atha yan madhor apāṃ vā eṣa oṣadhīnāṃ rasaḥ | [MS, 4, 4, 1 25]
apāṃ vā etad oṣadhīnāṃ rasena rāṣṭre rasaṃ dadhāti | [MS, 4, 4, 1 26]
ṣoḍaśa vā ete grahāḥ prājāpatyāḥ | [MS, 4, 4, 1 27]
samānītaḥ saptadaśaḥ | [MS, 4, 4, 1 28]
prajāpatiḥ saptadaśaḥ | [MS, 4, 4, 1 29]
prajāpatim evāpnoti | [MS, 4, 4, 1 30]
{MS, 4, 4, 2}
devīr āpo madhumatīḥ saṃsṛjyadhvaṃ mahi kṣatraṃ kṣatriyāya vanvānā iti | [MS, 4, 4, 2 1.1]
etā hi kṣatrasya vantrīḥ | [MS, 4, 4, 2 1.2]

anibhṛṣṭam asīti | [MS, 4, 4, 2 1.5]

tapojā iti | [MS, 4, 4, 2 1.7]

āyur vai hiraṇyam | [MS, 4, 4, 2 1.11]
āyuṣyā evainā akaḥ | [MS, 4, 4, 2 1.12]

devo vaḥ savitā punātv achidreṇa pavitreṇeti | [MS, 4, 4, 2 1.15]
etad vā achidraṃ pavitraṃ yat sūryasya raśmayaḥ | [MS, 4, 4, 2 1.16]
achidreṇaivaināḥ pavitreṇa punāti | [MS, 4, 4, 2 1.17]
svāhā rājasūyā iti | [MS, 4, 4, 2 1.18]
rājasūyā hy etāḥ | [MS, 4, 4, 2 1.19]
sadhamādo dyumnyā ūrjā ekā iti vyānayati vāruṇyā | [MS, 4, 4, 2 1.20]
vāruṇīr hy āpaḥ | [MS, 4, 4, 2 1.21]
svayaiva devatayā | [MS, 4, 4, 2 1.22]
rudra yat te giriparaṃ nāmeti | [MS, 4, 4, 2 1.23]
rudram evāsmāt tena niravadayate | [MS, 4, 4, 2 1.24]
tasmin hutam asi yameṣṭam asi svāheti | [MS, 4, 4, 2 1.25]
mṛtyur vai yamaḥ | [MS, 4, 4, 2 1.26]
mṛtyum evāsmāt tena niravadayate | [MS, 4, 4, 2 1.27]

tad vāva suśravā yat tad aśṛṇot | [MS, 4, 4, 2 1.33]
parṇamayenābhiṣiñcati | [MS, 4, 4, 2 1.34]
brahmābhiṣiñcati | [MS, 4, 4, 2 1.35]

atho brahma vai brahmā | [MS, 4, 4, 2 1.37]

viśo vīryam apākrāmat | [MS, 4, 4, 2 1.39]
tad aśvatthaṃ prāviśat | [MS, 4, 4, 2 1.40]
sa tena vīryeṇa bharbharābhavat | [MS, 4, 4, 2 1.41]
tad viśa evaitena vīryam avarunddhe | [MS, 4, 4, 2 1.42]
audumbareṇa bhrātṛvye | [MS, 4, 4, 2 1.43]
ūrg vā udumbaraḥ | [MS, 4, 4, 2 1.44]
